According to #EC @ecfin simulations, GDP would be more than 6 percentage points higher after 10 years, relative to a non-reform scenario.
#ECOFIN discussed the positive impact of structural reforms on the GDP of the EU economies. #Riga #EC #EuropeanSemester
This growth strategy should be based on three main priorities: investment, structural reforms and fiscal responsibility. #ECOFIN
Recovery in the euro area is strengthening, but still is fragile. The EU countries should implement a coordinated growth strategy. #ECOFIN
#ECOFIN #Riga focused on how to raise the growth potential in the EU, notably through structural #reforms and #investment. #EU #EC

My speech at @CES_Harvard @Harvard http://t.co/IAImNpLEmT Thanks to @chrisketels for steering the discussion http://t.co/RAUoteI4dt
With the US, EU shares a vision of democracy, prosperity & peace. Together we can recover. Together we're greater than the sum of our parts.
#EU and #US should take joint action to support #Ukraine in its efforts to build a secure, stable and economically developed country.
#Minsk should be fully implemented by all parties, to avoid a risk of further escalation of the conflict. #EU & #US must not let this happen

#TTIP - it is important to address the diversification of energy supply sources by ensuring access to #US gas and crude oil. @CES_Harvard
Stricking a deal on #TTIP would help #EU and #US to facilitate global recovery and growth together @Harvard @CES_Harvard
We can make big gains by tackling the remaining barriers to trade between the EU and US - #TTIP is an important opportunity for both sides.
The EU and US are already each other‚Äôs biggest markets when it comes to trade. The volume of trade between us is over ‚Ç¨720 billion a year.
Deeper integration of #EMU: any further risk-sharing needs to go hand-in-hand with increased decision-making powers at the European level
For the longer term, we need to forge a common understanding of what is missing in the institutional architecture for a robust #EMU @Harvard
#EMU: several elements already in place ‚Äì strengthened economic governance framework, financial backstops, incl. ESM & the Banking Union.
With deeper Economic and Monetary Union, Europe will stand stronger against future shocks. It's also the path to a real economic convergence
Creation of Capital Markets Union will help to strengthen the role of capital markets in financing the real economy @CES_Harvard
To diversify sources of financing for the real economy, in addition to bank lending, we should work 2 provide financing from capital markets
This growth strategy is based on three main priorities: investment, structural reforms and fiscal responsibility. @CES_Harvard
The strength of Europe's recovery will depend on our Member States putting in place a common growth strategy @CES_Harvard
Since the start of the crisis, the ECB has gradually expanded its activities - as the Fed & other Central Banks around the globe have done.
Btwn 2008 and the start of the Banking Union in October 2014, Europe's 120 largest banking groups raised capital in excess of EUR250 billion
Banking Union has bail-in as a main principle of bank resolution reducing the risks for EU taxpayers to foot the bill if banks make mistakes
New financial backstops, ex. European Stability Mechanism - a firewall, providing loans 2 Euro countries in balance of payments difficulties
Fiscal and macroeconomic policies of the EU Member States are closely monitored. Recommendations are issued to correct identified imbalances
We now have an annual fiscal and macroeconomic governance mechanism ‚Äì called the #EuropeanSemester. @CES_Harvard
Europe has come a long way in reinforcing the economic policy coordination - new framework helps focusing minds http://t.co/X822yXM3C5
During the crisis, we had to tackle economic imbalances on ad hoc basis & create from scratch new economic govern. structures @CES_Harvard
The crisis exposed the economic weaknesses present in many EU countries & in the design of the Economic and Monetary Union. @CES_Harvard
Recovery from a deep crisis as the one we have seen requires decisive action from economic policy makers @CES_Harvard
